sp_dn_m1AauxQx sx_c97cd7"></i></span></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="_5pbx userContent" data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"><p>You eat with others. It&#039;s like a family style with people you just met. I was in excellent company. We talked and laughed a lot. Nice people. Great service. Tasty, well-prepared food. I had homemade Chicken soup, the catch of the day which was Cod that was accompanied by broccoli, rice, and chili. Dessert of Pound Cake with whip cream and coffee. 3-course meal for an asking donation of $10. If you decide to pay more, you&#039;re passing the extra payment on to someone who can&#039;t afford it. &quot;Paying it forward&quot;. Payment&#039;s not mandatory. If you can&#039;t pay, you can volunteer at the Soul Kitchen as your payment, and they do it discreetly. No one at the table will know if your paying or working the meal off. I&#039;m going back.</p><div class="_5wpt"></div></div><div class="_3x-2"><div data-ft="&#123;&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;H&quot;&#125;"></div></div></div><div><form rel="async" class="commentable_item"
